temp2m=>temp2m  0  t,y,x  temperature at 2m

dswf=>dswf  0  t,y,x  shortwave downwelling radiative flux at the surface
dlwf=>dlwf  0  t,y,x  longwave downwelling radiative flux at the surface
ttend=>ttend  15  t,z,y,x  temperature tendency associated to the total radiative flux divergence
temp=>temp  15  t,z,y,x  temperature
rh=>rh  15  t,z,y,x  relative humidity
endvars
